## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) expression is:
$$-0.6057(T - 298.0) + \epsilon \cdot 3.1474 \cdot \exp(-(T - 298.0)^2)$$

This has two key structural features:
1. A **linear term in T** (with no epsilon dependence): $-c_0 T + c_0 c_1$
2. A term that is **linear in epsilon** multiplied by $\exp(-(T-c_3)^2)$, which is a **Gaussian function of T**

The critical challenge is finding a candidate that can produce $\epsilon \cdot \exp(-(T - c_3)^2)$, which is a Gaussian in T multiplied by epsilon.

Let me examine the candidates:

**Most candidates** have structures involving:
- `exp(c*epsilon)` — exponential in epsilon, not T
- `sin(c*epsilon + c)` — sinusoidal in epsilon
- `exp(c/T)` — exponential of 1/T, not a Gaussian in T
- `log(T*c + ...)` — logarithmic in T
- Polynomial terms in epsilon and T

**None of the candidates contain `exp(-T**2)` or any form that could produce a Gaussian in T.** The GT requires $\exp(-(T-c)^2) = \exp(-T^2 + 2cT - c^2)$, which is a Gaussian bell curve in T. This cannot be represented by:
- `exp(c/T)` (which is an inverse-T exponential)
- `exp(c*epsilon)` (exponential in epsilon, not T)
- `log(T*c + 1)` (logarithmic)
- `T**c` (power law)
- `sin(...)` (periodic)
- Any polynomial in T

I checked every candidate systematically:
- Candidates 1-50 all lack any term of the form `exp(-T^2)` or `exp(-(T-c)^2)`.
- The epsilon-dependent Gaussian-in-T term $\epsilon \cdot \exp(-(T-298)^2)$ is structurally impossible to reproduce with any of the available functional forms.

Even the linear-in-T part ($-0.6057T + 180.5$) can be matched by many candidates, but the Gaussian-in-T term multiplied by epsilon cannot be produced by any candidate formula, regardless of parameter choices.

Conclusion: No match
